# Comments for Question 4, LLM=Gemini 2.0 Flash Exp

== Grader: Claude 3.7 Sonnet ==
  * grade_story_101.txt (grade=3.1)
    The story attempts philosophical depth but undermines itself through repetition and lack of narrative progression. The bee pin symbolism shows potential but isn't developed beyond surface-level explanation. The story tells rather than shows its themes about adaptation and resilience, with no emotional stakes or conflict to engage the reader.

  * grade_story_104.txt (grade=6.5)
    The story effectively uses the miniature worlds as metaphors for societal control, with the encrypted labels representing subversive communication. The central theme of quiet rebellion against conformity emerges clearly. However, the story relies too heavily on telling rather than showing, with abstract statements about "defiance" and "freedom" instead of concrete, specific moments that demonstrate these concepts in action.

The metaphor of the lamp as broken vows shows promise, but the story's impact is diminished by predictable progression and somewhat generic imagery.
